#[derive(Eq, PartialEq, Hash, Debug)]
pub enum RegistryKey {
    BannerPattern,
    Block,
    DamageType,
    Dialog,
    Enchantment,
    EntityType,
    Fluid,
    GameEvent,
    Instrument,
    Item,
    PaintingVariant,
    PointOfInterestType,
    WorldgenBiome,
}
impl RegistryKey {
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn identifier_string(&self) -> &str {
        match self {
            Self::BannerPattern => "banner_pattern",
            Self::Block => "block",
            Self::DamageType => "damage_type",
            Self::Dialog => "dialog",
            Self::Enchantment => "enchantment",
            Self::EntityType => "entity_type",
            Self::Fluid => "fluid",
            Self::GameEvent => "game_event",
            Self::Instrument => "instrument",
            Self::Item => "item",
            Self::PaintingVariant => "painting_variant",
            Self::PointOfInterestType => "point_of_interest_type",
            Self::WorldgenBiome => "worldgen/biome",
        }
    }
}
pub type Tag = (&'static [&'static str], &'static [u16]);
#[allow(non_snake_case)]

    use crate::tag::Tag;
    pub const MINECRAFT_NO_ITEM_REQUIRED: Tag = (

pub fn get_tag_values(tag_category: RegistryKey, tag: &str) -> Option<&'static [&'static str]> {
    match tag_category {
        RegistryKey::BannerPattern => BANNERPATTERN_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Block => BLOCK_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::DamageType => DAMAGETYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Dialog => DIALOG_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Enchantment => ENCHANTMENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::EntityType => ENTITYTYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Fluid => FLUID_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::GameEvent => GAMEEVENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Instrument => INSTRUMENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::Item => ITEM_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::PaintingVariant => PAINTINGVARIANT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::PointOfInterestType => POINTOFINTERESTTYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
        RegistryKey::WorldgenBiome => WORLDGENBIOME_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.0),
    }
}
pub fn get_tag_ids(tag_category: RegistryKey, tag: &str) -> Option<&'static [u16]> {
    match tag_category {
        RegistryKey::BannerPattern => BANNERPATTERN_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Block => BLOCK_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::DamageType => DAMAGETYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Dialog => DIALOG_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Enchantment => ENCHANTMENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::EntityType => ENTITYTYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Fluid => FLUID_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::GameEvent => GAMEEVENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Instrument => INSTRUMENT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::Item => ITEM_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::PaintingVariant => PAINTINGVARIANT_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::PointOfInterestType => POINTOFINTERESTTYPE_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
        RegistryKey::WorldgenBiome => WORLDGENBIOME_TAGS.get(tag).map(|i| i.1),
    }
}
pub fn get_registry_key_tags(tag_category: &RegistryKey) -> &phf::Map<&'static str, &'static Tag> {
    match tag_category {
        RegistryKey::BannerPattern => &BANNERPATTERN_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Block => &BLOCK_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::DamageType => &DAMAGETYPE_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Dialog => &DIALOG_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Enchantment => &ENCHANTMENT_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::EntityType => &ENTITYTYPE_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Fluid => &FLUID_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::GameEvent => &GAMEEVENT_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Instrument => &INSTRUMENT_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::Item => &ITEM_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::PaintingVariant => &PAINTINGVARIANT_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::PointOfInterestType => &POINTOFINTERESTTYPE_TAGS,
        RegistryKey::WorldgenBiome => &WORLDGENBIOME_TAGS,
    }
}
pub trait Taggable {
    fn tag_key() -> RegistryKey;
    fn registry_key(&self) -> &str;
    fn registry_id(&self) -> u16;
    #[doc = r" Returns `None` if the tag does not exist."]
    fn is_tagged_with(&self, tag: &str) -> Option<bool> {
        let tag = tag.strip_prefix("#").unwrap_or(tag);
        let items = get_tag_ids(Self::tag_key(), tag)?;
        Some(items.contains(&self.registry_id()))
    }
    fn is_tagged_with_by_tag(&self, tag: &'static Tag) -> bool {
        tag.1.contains(&self.registry_id())
    }
    fn get_tag_values(tag: &str) -> Option<&'static [&'static str]> {
        let tag = tag.strip_prefix("#").unwrap_or(tag);
        get_tag_values(Self::tag_key(), tag)
    }
}
